#### Logo Variations

**1. Primary Logo (Full)**
```
[Icon] + CINEVERSE (horizontal)
- Sá»­ dá»¥ng cho header, marketing materials
- KÃ­ch thÆ°á»›c tá»‘i thiá»ƒu: 120px width
```

**2. Logo with Tagline**
```
[Icon] + CINEVERSE
"Your Universe of Cinema"
- Sá»­ dá»¥ng cho landing pages, about pages
```

**3. Icon Only (Favicon/App Icon)**
```
[Icon] only
- Sá»­ dá»¥ng cho favicon, mobile app icon, social media avatar
- KÃ­ch thÆ°á»›c: 16x16, 32x32, 48x48, 192x192, 512x512
```

**4. Wordmark Only**
```
CINEVERSE (text only)
- Sá»­ dá»¥ng khi khÃ´ng gian háº¡n cháº¿
- Footer, watermarks
```

**5. Monochrome Versions**
```
- White on dark: Cho dark mode
- Black on light: Cho light mode
- Grayscale: Cho in áº¥n Ä‘en tráº¯ng
```

#### Logo Specifications

```
COLORS:
- Primary Gradient: #DC2626 (Red) â†’ #EAB308 (Gold)
- Solid Red: #DC2626
- Solid Gold: #EAB308
- White: #FFFFFF
- Dark: #18181B

TYPOGRAPHY (Wordmark):
- Font: Cinzel Decorative (hoáº·c Playfair Display)
- Weight: Bold (700)
- Letter Spacing: 0.15em (wider)
- Style: All Caps

ICON PROPORTIONS:
- Icon height = 1x
- Wordmark height = 0.4x
- Spacing between icon and wordmark = 0.2x
- Clear space around logo = 0.5x (minimum)

MINIMUM SIZES:
- Full logo: 120px width
- Icon only: 24px
- Favicon: 16x16px
```

#### Logo Usage Guidelines

```
âœ… DO:
- Use on dark backgrounds for best impact
- Maintain aspect ratio
- Use approved color variations
- Keep clear space around logo

âŒ DON'T:
- Stretch or distort
- Use on busy backgrounds without contrast
- Change colors outside brand palette
- Add effects (shadows, outlines) not in brand guide
- Place text too close to logo
```

## 3. DESIGN PHILOSOPHY - TRIáº¾T LÃ THIáº¾T Káº¾

### 3.1 Aesthetic Direction: "Cinematic Elegance"

```
CONCEPT: "Premium Cinema Experience at Home"

Káº¿t há»£p 3 yáº¿u tá»‘:
1. LUXURY/REFINED - Sang trá»ng, tinh táº¿
   - MÃ u sáº¯c Ä‘áº­m, contrast cao
   - Typography thanh lá»‹ch
   - Negative space rá»™ng rÃ£i
   
2. EDITORIAL/MAGAZINE - TrÃ¬nh bÃ y nhÆ° táº¡p chÃ­ cao cáº¥p
   - Layout asymmetric, grid-breaking
   - Typography hierarchy rÃµ rÃ ng
   - Feature content prominently
   
3. CINEMATIC/DRAMATIC - Äiá»‡n áº£nh, ká»‹ch tÃ­nh
   - Dark mode dominant
   - Lighting effects (glow, gradients)
   - Immersive imagery
```

### 3.2 Design Principles

```
1. IMMERSIVE FIRST
   - Content (phim) lÃ  trung tÃ¢m
   - UI "biáº¿n máº¥t" khi xem phim
   - Backgrounds há»— trá»£, khÃ´ng cáº¡nh tranh

2. DRAMATIC CONTRAST
   - Dark backgrounds vá»›i bright accents
   - Text hierarchy rÃµ rÃ ng
   - Focus states ná»•i báº­t

3. FLUID MOTION
   - Transitions mÆ°á»£t mÃ 
   - Micro-interactions tinh táº¿
   - Loading states elegant

4. ACCESSIBLE LUXURY
   - Sang trá»ng nhÆ°ng dá»… sá»­ dá»¥ng
   - Touch targets Ä‘á»§ lá»›n
   - Readable at all sizes
```

### 3.3 Visual Mood Board

```
INSPIRATION SOURCES:
â”œâ”€â”€ Netflix Premium Tier (layout, navigation)
â”œâ”€â”€ Apple TV+ (typography, elegance)
â”œâ”€â”€ MUBI (editorial approach)
â”œâ”€â”€ IMDb (information density)

â””â”€â”€ Luxury Hotel Websites (refinement)

KEY VISUAL ELEMENTS:
â”œâ”€â”€ Film grain texture overlays
â”œâ”€â”€ Vignette effects on hero images
â”œâ”€â”€ Soft glow effects on accent elements
â”œâ”€â”€ Gradient meshes for depth
â”œâ”€â”€ Glass morphism for overlays
â””â”€â”€ Subtle noise textures
```

### 3.4 Unique Design Features

```
1. "CURTAIN REVEAL" ANIMATION
   - Page transitions nhÆ° má»Ÿ mÃ n ráº¡p hÃ¡t
   - Content reveals tá»« center ra ngoÃ i
   
2. "SPOTLIGHT" HOVER EFFECT
   - Cards Ä‘Æ°á»£c "chiáº¿u sÃ¡ng" khi hover
   - Subtle light beam effect
   
3. "FILM STRIP" NAVIGATION
   - Horizontal scrolling nhÆ° cuá»™n phim
   - Perforation marks decoration
   
4. "GOLDEN RATIO" LAYOUTS
   - Sá»­ dá»¥ng tá»‰ lá»‡ vÃ ng cho compositions
   - Asymmetric nhÆ°ng balanced

Dark Theme Usage:
- 950: Page background (deepest)
- 900: Card backgrounds, sections
- 800: Elevated surfaces, inputs
- 700: Borders, dividers
- 500-600: Muted text
- 300-400: Secondary text
- 50-100: Primary text (white)
```

## 10. ANIMATION & MOTION DESIGN

### 10.1 Animation Principles

```
1. PURPOSE-DRIVEN
   - Má»—i animation pháº£i cÃ³ má»¥c Ä‘Ã­ch rÃµ rÃ ng
   - HÆ°á»›ng dáº«n user attention
   - Feedback cho actions

2. CINEMATIC TIMING
   - Sá»­ dá»¥ng easings phÃ¹ há»£p vá»›i "cinematic" feel
   - KhÃ´ng quÃ¡ nhanh (rushed), khÃ´ng quÃ¡ cháº­m (sluggish)
   - 200-500ms lÃ  sweet spot

3. CONSISTENCY
   - CÃ¹ng loáº¡i animation cho cÃ¹ng loáº¡i action
   - Stagger delays nháº¥t quÃ¡n
   - Easing functions nháº¥t quÃ¡n

4. RESPECT PREFERENCES
   - Support prefers-reduced-motion
   - Fallback cho low-end devices
```

### 10.2 Animation Specifications

```

â”‚                                                              â”‚

â”‚  ease-in:         cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)               â”‚
â”‚  ease-in-out:     cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)             â”‚
â”‚  cinematic-out:   cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1)            â”‚
â”‚  cinematic-in:    cubic-bezier(0.7, 0, 0.84, 0)            â”‚
â”‚  bounce:          cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55)   â”‚

## 14. DELIVERABLES CHECKLIST

### Design Assets to Create:

```
â˜ BRAND IDENTITY
  â˜ Logo (all variations)
  â˜ Favicon set
  â˜ Social media kit
  â˜ Brand guidelines document

â˜ DESIGN SYSTEM
  â˜ Color palette (with all shades)
  â˜ Typography scale
  â˜ Spacing system
  â˜ Shadow system
  â˜ Border radius system
  â˜ Icon set

â˜ COMPONENT LIBRARY
  â˜ Buttons (all variants, states)
  â˜ Form elements
  â˜ Cards (movie, thumbnail, featured)
  â˜ Navigation components
  â˜ Modal & overlays
  â˜ Video player
  â˜ Loading states
  â˜ Empty states
  â˜ Error states

â˜ PAGE DESIGNS (Desktop + Tablet + Mobile)
  â˜ Homepage
  â˜ Movie detail page
  â˜ Watch page
  â˜ Search/Filter page
  â˜ Category page
  â˜ Actor/Director page
  â˜ Watchlist page
  â˜ History page
  â˜ Settings page
  â˜ Static pages (About, Contact, Terms, Privacy)
  â˜ 404 & 500 error pages

â˜ ADMIN DASHBOARD (Desktop + Tablet)
  â˜ Dashboard home
  â˜ Films list
  â˜ Film edit form
  â˜ Crawler management
  â˜ Reports/Analytics
  â˜ Settings

â˜ PROTOTYPES & INTERACTIONS
  â˜ Page transitions
  â˜ Component interactions
  â˜ Video player prototype
  â˜ Search flow

â˜ RESPONSIVE DESIGNS
  â˜ Mobile versions of all pages
  â˜ Tablet versions
  â˜ Large screen adaptations
